Guangdong Province Launches Major Arrests of Communist Bandits in Various Regions 68

Guangzhou Captures and Executes 20 Communist Bandits

N雄 and Shaoguan Successively Uncover Five Organizations

Guangzhou Correspondence - Since the large-scale suppression of communist bandits in Hunan and Jiangxi, the Guangdong authorities have also ordered the military and police in various regions to secretly implement a state of alert, strictly guarding against communists, and inspecting gun permits. In Guangzhou, the Public Security Bureau recently uncovered a communist organization in a certain area, capturing 20 young communist bandits. After strict interrogation, they were sentenced to death. At around 5:00 PM on the 15th, the bureau dispatched two armored prison vans to escort them to the Honghuagang execution ground. Dozens of security team members were deployed along the way in cars for escort, and one supervising officer rode in a car at the rear. The situation was extremely serious. However, more than ten young male prisoners and several female prisoners in the prison vans sang songs along the way. Upon arriving at the execution ground, the security team members were divided to guard the area, and the prisoners were brought out one by one for execution by firing squad. The execution was completed at around 6:00 PM, and the team withdrew. In the Beijiang area, communist organizations have also been uncovered in N雄 and Shaoguan. Recently, Wu, the magistrate of N雄 County, reported that communist elements were hiding in Datang and Guozhu in the county. He immediately sent troops to search the villages near the area and found a large bundle of reactionary propaganda materials and several documents in the village houses. Several communist bandits were arrested on the spot and taken back to the county. The magistrate immediately telegraphed the provincial authorities for instructions. The authorities telegraphed back, ordering that the evidence against the confirmed criminals be executed on the spot, and the seized propaganda materials be sent for filing. Furthermore, the Third Independent Regiment of the Shaoguan garrison also uncovered several communist organizations in Shaoguan at the beginning of the month. Previously, the regimental commander received intelligence that the general communist organization in Dongjiang had sent dozens of elements from Wuhua and Xingning to Beijiang to collude with local communist bandits and take the opportunity to mobilize disreputable soldiers, plotting a riot on Sun Yat-sen's birthday. In addition to ordering strict precautions, the regiment secretly ordered its subordinates to play along, catching all the bandits at once. On the 8th, communist bandits arrived at a certain company headquarters in Shaoguan to mobilize more than ten soldiers, and a total of seven or eight communist bandits held a secret meeting in the company. The regiment headquarters discovered the meeting and immediately dispatched troops to surround the area, arresting more than twenty people and taking them to the regimental headquarters for interrogation. It was learned that the general communist organization was located at the Shaoguan North Gate Slaughterhouse. The next day (9th), the Third Independent Regiment again searched the address and found a large number of reactionary propaganda materials and more than thirty handguns at the general organization, arresting more than twenty criminals. After interrogation, it was learned that the communist bandits were sent by Dongjiang to incite soldiers and collude with local communists to seize a corner of Beijiang to respond to the Zhu and Peng factions in Hunan and Jiangxi. The regimental commander and the soldiers of the regiment remained calm and dispatched troops again the next day to disarm the machine gun company. On the 11th, another communist organization was uncovered at the South Gate, and the party's proposals and many anti-insurgency banners were found. A total of four organizations were uncovered in the past few days. Five principal offenders were arrested and executed outside the North Gate of Shaoguan City on the 14th. More than twenty remaining arrested bandits and more than ten suspects are still under interrogation, and efforts are being made to capture the fugitives to eliminate the roots. (November 18th)

The Trend of Relaxing the Ban on Silver Exports in Shantou

Inside Story: Originated from Speculation in Singapore Currency Notes 69

Shantou Correspondence: Last year, due to the remittance of silver by overseas Chinese in Nanyang, various banks in Shantou transported a large amount of cash from Shanghai for the purpose of exchanging silver notes. This year, due to the high gold prices, cash from rural areas has been absorbed and transported out, amounting to more than one thousand taels of silver per day. The use of cash has therefore become more widespread. The remaining cash in Shantou City is nearly ten million. The situation changes with the times, and things are not always abundant. As the prices of Nanyang rubber and tin have fallen, the exchange of notes in Shantou has sharply decreased. The cash hidden among the people is also almost exhausted. However, this large amount of cash is still in the Shantou market. There are more than three hundred silver exchange firms in Shantou, which, in addition to lending money at interest, also buy and sell Singapore notes, Hong Kong notes, and central bank notes. Recently, the trend of speculating in Singapore notes has become very popular, and the market is like a drunkard. Guangxing Zhuang is the leader of the buyers, and Jiacheng Zhuang is the leader of the sellers. The daily trading volume reaches more than one million yuan. The buyers benefit from rising prices, while the sellers benefit from falling prices. Each side tries its best to manipulate the market due to their conflicting interests. The lifting of the ban on silver exports is a quick way to succeed in selling Singapore notes. Because exporting silver to Hong Kong and Xiamen can bring a profit of twenty yuan per thousand yuan, the cash in the market is depleted, and the daily interest rate can be increased. Since the ban was lifted, the daily interest rate has risen from eight percent to twenty-four percent in just a few days. After the silver supply is shaken, many merchants sell notes to be exchanged elsewhere, and the price of the notes will inevitably fall, which is another benefit for silver firms. As the price of notes falls everywhere, the price of Singapore notes will inevitably decrease, and the buyers will suffer significant losses. The advantages and disadvantages of commercial warfare are such that anyone with basic economic knowledge can see it, but the authorities are ignorant and do not understand. Therefore, since the ban was lifted, Jiacheng, Yucheng, Hongkang, Jiade, and other firms have been exporting hundreds of thousands of yuan every day. More than ten merchants selling Shantou, Suzhou, Guangdong, northern and southern seafood have sent telegrams of opposition, and newspapers have published articles criticizing them. Many silver firms secretly laugh because they have achieved great success within a dozen days of the ban being lifted, and it does not matter if the ban is reimposed. Seeing that the trend of exporting silver is like a river flowing downhill, Luo Zongmeng, the Customs Superintendent, has ordered that anyone transporting more than five thousand yuan of silver must obtain a passport before being allowed to export it, slightly restricting it. The rise of these trends and opposition from the southern economic community is very significant and cannot be ignored. (17th)

British Sailing Ship "Corley" Encountered Danger

Ran Aground Outside Shantou Harbor 70

Two Englishmen Rescued by Fishing Boat 71

Shantou Correspondence: Europeans and Americans are brave and curious. Anyone who has read "Robinson Crusoe" or "Newspaper Reporter" can understand this. Last month, a wealthy British merchant from Tianjin named Moore-Murong, with tens of millions of assets and nearly ancient age, with gray hair and beard, still wanted to brave the waves and explore the Chinese coastline. Mr. Moore specially made a large sailing ship named "Corley." The ship was forty-six feet long and twelve feet wide, with two masts that could hoist sails and sail along the coastline. The ship was divided into six cabins, storing sufficient food and supplies. The entire ship was manufactured to be extremely sturdy and skillful. On October 1st, he set off from Tianjin with a navigator (also British). On the 20th, he arrived safely outside Wusongkou, Shanghai. On the 23rd, he departed from Shanghai and headed south, intending to reach Guangzhou Bay or Guangzhou as the final destination. Unexpectedly, when he arrived at the Xiamen sea area, the rudder was suddenly damaged by the waves, but it could still barely support sailing. On November 5th, he sailed into the Xingyu area of Shantou's territorial waters. This area is surrounded by mountains with hidden reefs, which have always been the location of shipwrecks. The "Corley" could not avoid this, and the ship's hull hit sharp reefs, and the entire ship sank. Fortunately, there were fishing boats fishing in groups in the area, and the two Englishmen were rescued by the fishermen. On the 9th, they were brought to Shantou. Moore-Murong and the other were exposed to the wind and sun, their faces were dark, their beards were messy, and their clothes were torn. Those who saw them almost thought they were beggars. Moore and others went to see the Customs Commissioner of Shantou Customs and told him the situation. The Customs Commissioner then learned that he was a giant merchant with courage and bravery. He then helped them stay at the Wolong Hotel in front of the Customs and telegraphed their firm in Tianjin to remit money to Shantou to welcome them back. (11th)

Recent Situation and Preliminary Plans for the Longhai Railway (Continued) 72

Work Status (1) Status of the Project: The completed route extends from Dapu in the east to Lingbao in the west, a total of 825 kilometers. Due to the incomplete equipment during the construction period and the frequent turbulent situation over the years, the project has been greatly affected. The project funds are insufficient, and the materials are lacking. The condition of the tracks is deteriorating day by day. The 88 kilometers from the 452nd kilometer east of Xin'anzhen to Dapu have not yet been laid with ballast. The rails and sleepers are directly laid on the soil base, which has been for more than four years. The sleepers are extremely easy to rot, and there is a danger of driving. It has been delayed until now and urgently needs to be rectified. In addition, the protection dike project between the Grand Canal and Haizhou has not yet been carried out. Moreover, since the 15th year of the Republic of China, there have been very few replacements of sleepers along the road. According to the latest survey, there are about 210,000 decayed sleepers on the entire line, accounting for 25% of the total number of sleepers. Although the current driving speed is strictly limited, the possibility of danger still exists and needs to be planned. (2) Equipment along the Road: The equipment on this line is simple due to the unfinished project. The signal shapes and turnout signals that should be available at each station have not been installed. The equipment for locomotive water supply is also incomplete. Water supply is already lacking in peacetime, and military transportation is even more difficult. The equipment such as mileage and gradient signs along the road is even more irrelevant. (3) Damage from the War: Since the Northwest Army retreated from Xishan west to Luoyang in May, more than thirty large and small bridges along the line have been bombed. Only more than ten small bridges have been officially repaired. The rest are temporarily built with temporary detours or supported with sleepers and wooden frames to facilitate traffic. During this campaign against the rebels, fighting has been going on along the line for more than six months, from February 8th to October 10th. Seventy-six bridges have been bombed. The number of rails, sleepers, and turnout devices at various stations that have been dismantled and bombed along the way is even more difficult to count. About a dozen houses have been destroyed along the way, and the houses at Minquan Station have been completely destroyed. The amount of damage and the size of the loss are estimated to be over one million. (4) Preparation and Restoration of Engineering Materials: The materials for this line were extremely scarce. As soon as the current military affairs began, an engineering train was organized to load all the required materials and tools, and a hundred experienced workers were selected and led by the supervisor to advance with the army. On the one hand, it was negotiated with the Jinpu Railway to transfer 15,000 sleepers. Later, funds were raised to purchase 9,560 sleepers from Mitsui Yangxing. Finally, Jinpu was entrusted to purchase 10,000 foreign pine sleepers. Fortunately, this material repair project was not delayed. Steel rails, turnouts, and other items were temporarily borrowed from the Western Route Engineering Bureau to meet emergency needs. The remaining scattered materials were either purchased locally or self-made by the road in order to avoid delaying the repair project. (5) Situation of Repair: The engineering train organized by this line has always been advancing with the army. Any damage is repaired immediately. Sometimes, even under the line of fire, they work at night and without stopping, never delaying military affairs. All bombed rails and turnouts have been replaced. The destroyed bridges are temporarily supported with sleepers. Steel beams that hinder traffic are either sawed or dismantled to ensure that traffic can be restored in the shortest possible time. The repairs between Kaifeng and Zhengzhou are even faster. Two or three hours after the recapture of Zhengzhou, the engineering vehicle repaired along the road in the rain of bullets and bombs, and bravely advanced, so it was able to reach the station first. Now the rails and bridges between Zhengzhou and Lingbao have also been repaired and will be open to traffic immediately.

Vehicle Operations (1) Situation in the Initial Period: In February of this year, all the vehicles on this line were seized by Han Shiren's and other departments, and less than twenty vehicles could be freely used. After repeated negotiations, about 280 vehicles were returned one after another. In addition to those requisitioned by the Transportation Headquarters for military use, the most for this line's business was about 100 vehicles, and the least was only 20 to 30 vehicles. On average, about 50 to 60 vehicles were used to maintain operations for several months. (2) Situation of Military Transportation: Military transportation lasted only nine months from February to October. The return of the army must be completed in November, which is not yet included. During wartime, due to strategic relations, whether advancing or retreating, the busyness of transportation is indescribable. In August and September, the number of military trains reached more than 490 times. In total, from February to the end of September, a total of 2,667 military trains were operated, totaling 227,619 train kilometers. (3) Situation of Passenger Transport: The first and second passenger and freight trains between Xuzhou and Dapu have been operating normally since February. Only two third-class passenger cars are attached, and a number of freight cars are attached to facilitate the flow of goods. The order in this section is still good because there is no war. The third and fourth passenger and freight trains west of Xuzhou opened to Neihuang in February, to Minquan in March, to Dangshan in April, and to Shangqiu from May to September. From October 7th, they resumed their original status and opened to Zhengzhou. From October 14th, the fifth and sixth passenger and freight trains between Zhengzhou and Luoyang operated as usual. However, since military transportation has not yet completely ended, it is difficult to accurately determine the train schedule. In total, passenger transport revenue from February to the end of September was about 120,000 yuan. (4) Situation of Freight Transport: Since the outbreak of the war, traffic has been blocked, and the source of goods west of Shangqiu has been cut off. The maintenance relies on the export of wheat, peanuts, and other miscellaneous grains from Dangshan, Huangkou, Tongshan, Xuzhou, and other stations. The imports are miscellaneous goods from Dapu. The salt from Huaibei is transported by sea to Nankou and then transported by the Jinpu Railway to Bengbu. In order to facilitate merchants, a method of transporting salt directly to Bengbu was planned and approved by the Ministry. Since the implementation of this method, it only takes twenty hours from Haizhou to Bengbu, and merchants praise it. In total, from February to the end of September, 128 full freight trains were operated, 16 trains of Zhongxing coal were operated, and 23 trains of salt were operated, totaling 27,884 train kilometers, with a revenue of about 800,000 yuan. (5) Matters that Urgently Need to be Rectified and Equipped: This line has huge debts and simple equipment. After this period of military affairs, the trauma is even deeper. If we do not urgently seek to rectify and increase revenue, how can we fund the injection? On the vehicle operations side, the current plans include: 1. Restoring the special express train between Xuzhou and Zhengzhou and the passenger and freight trains on the entire line. 2. Unblocking accumulated goods and absorbing new goods, focusing on eliminating malpractices and providing convenience. 3. Rectifying and equipping the telegraph and telephone lines on the entire line. 4. Installing electric and gas line signs to ensure traffic safety. These are all symptomatic treatments. As for the fundamental method, the plan will be determined after the overall plan.

Regulations of the Anti-Opium Association on the Method of Burning Opium 73

The Central Anti-Opium Committee previously approved a letter from the Jinling Customs Salt Supervision Office stating that from October 1st to November 4th of this year, a total of 4,980 taels of opium and 128 taels of fake opium drugs were seized. It was decided to publicly burn them at Xiaguan on November 8th and requested to send personnel to supervise. The committee then sent staff member Yang Shusheng as a representative to supervise. According to the reply, the representatives of various agencies weighed the opium in person on that day and found that the opium was genuine. The genuine opium, including the wrapping, weighed 345 catties, excluding 15 catties, the net weight of the opium was 330 catties, equivalent to 5,280 taels, which was more than 300 taels more than the above number. There was deep suspicion, and the representative of the customs was immediately asked. According to the statement, the customs estimated that the weight of the wrapping was about 4,980 taels when it was seized, checked, weighed, and estimated by the customs. It was found that this kind of estimate has no fixed standard and is very likely to cause malpractices. The committee believes that the opium seized in various places is usually checked, weighed, and sealed by the responsible personnel before being publicly burned to show fairness. The customs' method of estimating the removal of packaging has no fixed standard and is prone to malpractices. Therefore, yesterday, a letter was sent to the Jinling Customs Superintendent requesting that the seized opium should be weighed, sealed, and stored by the responsible personnel without estimating the removal of the paper skin to show the truth. When it is scheduled to be burned, the representatives of various agencies will check the seal, open it, supervise the weighing, and then burn it to show great trust.

Implementation of Sericulture Administration in Jiangsu Province

Correcting the Organization of the Experiment Station 74

Establishing a Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant 75

Since the Agricultural Department decided to promote the three policies of silkworm breeding, silkworm egg improvement, and silk manufacturing improvement for sericulture improvement in Jiangsu Province, it has been planned to carry out them separately in the five years from the 17th to the 21st year. In November of the 18th year, the Provincial Sericulture Experiment Station was reorganized into the Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field, and the raw silkworm seed department of the original Yangzhou Sericulture Experiment Field was attached to the Sericulture Experiment Field. Now, the need for raw silkworm seeds is increasing day by day, and the planned route must be changed according to the times. Therefore, the original organizational regulations of the Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field were revised, and the Yangzhou Raw Silkworm Seed Department was divided into an independent entity named the Jiangsu Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant. The funding for this project is still allocated from the original funding of the Experiment Field. The revised Jiangsu Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field and the drafted organizational regulations of the Jiangsu Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant were submitted to the Provincial Government Committee for discussion yesterday (21st), and Tang Xixiang was recommended as the director of the Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant, which were all approved. The organizational regulations are recorded as follows:

Organizational Regulations of the Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field (Article 1) The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture, Mining and Commerce has established the Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field to promote the improvement of the silk industry in the province. (Article 2) The Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field is located in Wuxi. When necessary, branch fields may be established in various parts of the province. The regulations for branch fields shall be determined separately. (Article 3) The Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field shall have a director who shall be responsible for the affairs of the entire field and shall be recommended by the Department of Agriculture and Mining to the Provincial Government. (Article 4) The Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field shall have the following seven departments, each with a director who shall be responsible for the affairs of the department under the command of the director of the field: (1) Sericulture Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to silkworm breeding, matters related to raw silkworm seed manufacturing, matters related to silkworm breeding research. (2) Mulberry Cultivation Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to mulberry breeding, matters related to seedling cultivation, matters related to mulberry cultivation research. (3) Silk Manufacturing Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to silk quality investigation, matters related to silk manufacturing research, matters related to silk manufacturing training for women. (4) Sericulture Chemistry Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to sericulture chemistry research, matters related to silk chemistry research. (5) Silkworm Physiology and Pathology Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to silkworm physiology research, matters related to silkworm pathology research. (6) Promotion Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to publicity, matters related to introduction, matters related to guidance. (7) General Affairs Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to documents, matters related to accounting, matters related to general affairs, matters related to publication, matters that do not belong to other departments. (Article 5) The Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field shall have five to ten technicians, ten to twenty technical assistants, and a number of clerks and employees who shall be responsible for the affairs under their jurisdiction under the command of their superiors. (Article 6) The directors of each department and technicians of the Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field shall be selected by the director of the field and approved by the Department of Agriculture and Mining. The technical assistants, clerks, and employees shall be appointed or assigned by the director of the field and reported to the Department of Agriculture and Mining for record. (Article 7) The detailed rules for the Provincial Sericulture Experiment Field shall be determined separately. (Article 8) These regulations shall be implemented on the day of the resolution of the Provincial Government Committee meeting. Organizational Regulations of the Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant (Article 1) The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining has established the Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant to supply high-quality silkworm seeds and unify the quality of raw silk. (Article 2) The Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant is located in Yangzhou. (Article 3) The Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant shall have a director who shall be responsible for the affairs of the entire plant and shall be recommended by the Department of Agriculture and Mining to the Provincial Government. (Article 4) The Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant shall have the following three departments, each with a director who shall be responsible for the affairs of the department under the command of the director of the plant: 1. Seed Production Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to raw seed manufacturing, matters related to virus inspection. 2. Mulberry Orchard Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to seedling cultivation, matters related to mulberry orchard management. 3. General Affairs Department: Its responsibilities are as follows: matters related to documents and editing, matters related to accounting and general affairs, matters related to business contacts, matters that do not belong to other departments. (Article 5) The Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant shall have two to four technicians, six to ten technical assistants, and a number of clerks and employees who shall be responsible for the affairs under their jurisdiction under the command of their superiors. (Article 6) The directors of each department and technicians of the Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant shall be selected by the director of the plant and approved by the Department of Agriculture and Mining. The technical assistants, clerks, and employees shall be appointed or assigned by the director of the plant and reported to the Department of Agriculture and Mining for record. (Article 7) The detailed rules for the Provincial Raw Silkworm Seed Manufacturing Plant shall be determined separately. (Article 8) These regulations shall be implemented on the day of the resolution of the Provincial Government Committee meeting.

Jiangyin 81

Soil Traffickers Detained and Fined, Then Released: Huangtiangang Port, outside the North Gate, is a key thoroughfare for the Yangtze River, both upstream and downstream. The trafficking of opium is an open secret. Several seizures have been made this year, totaling 1400 catties, all transported to various ports in Jiangsu Province. The other day, Zhou Furong and Liu Kunsheng, stewards on the Dehe Steamer, transported 900 catties of opium intending to unload it in Nantong. However, several Jiangyin traffickers wanted to unload it in Cheng County. The stewards, wary of repeated incidents in Jiangyin, refused. The traffickers paid over 1,000 yuan in guarantees, and the stewards dumped the opium into the river. The ship sailed to Shanghai. Unexpectedly, the opium was discovered near Qiyu Port by a small vessel (affiliated with an unspecified organization). The traffickers were powerless to resist. Liu Fulao and others from the Dehe Steamer in Shanghai learned the news and came to Cheng County on the 18th to demand the opium from the traffickers, including Ge Laosi. On that day, a group of traffickers from other regions were gambling at Ge's house in Hexi when Cui Siping, chief of the First Public Security Precinct outside the North Gate, learned of it. He sent police to search Ge's house for opium but found nothing. He then took Ge Laosi and Chen Laoliu (both traffickers) to the precinct. After intervention from Shen Rongzhi, Cui fined the traffickers, 周福榮, etc., 55 yuan each, and Chen Laoliu 30 yuan each, releasing them on the night of the 19th. The matter was kept secret, and the Public Security Bureau and the County Government only learned of it yesterday. An investigation is planned.

Escaped Prisoner Apprehended in Shanghai and Escorted to Cheng County: Wu Biao of the Public Security Bureau's Detective Team learned on the 13th in Yongxing Road, Zhabei, Shanghai, that Zhu A'si (alias Wu Hongmou, also known as A'wu) and Xie Peizhi (alias Chun Geng) and two women, Jiang Jiaojiao and Zhu Shundi, from Zhulangzhong Bridge, Xixiang, Jiangyin, were hiding there. Zhu had committed a counter-revolutionary crime, robbing a cattle merchant of silver dollars and killing him, and was imprisoned but escaped on January 31st. This year, he participated in the Hong Kong robbery and assault on a police officer, and plotted to attack Cao Xiang, the chief of the Sixth District. Detective Wu immediately coordinated with the Fourth District Public Security to arrest them and escort them to the main bureau. He telegraphed the Jiangyin Public Security Bureau, and Detective Team Leader Yang Bingwei took a warrant to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau. According to Jiang Jiaojiao and Zhu Shundi, they were kidnapped by Zhu A'si and others in Zheng Dashu, Changzhou. They were sent to the Women and Children Relief Association for temporary care and the Wujin County Government was notified to investigate and summon the families of the women to the bureau to claim them. Zhu A'si and Xie Peizhi were handed over to Team Leader Yang and escorted to Cheng County on the 20th. Yang saw Xu Yourong, who was involved in the Jiangyin bandit case, at the North Station and also escorted him to Cheng County on the 21st. Today (the 22nd), they were separately handed over by the Public Security Bureau to the county for secret interrogation by Judge Yang Cheng and then ordered to be detained.

New Heng Da Steamer Sinks Xiehe Company's Zhenhuai Vessel: The New Heng Da steamer, en route from Zhenjiang, arrived near Wutai around 5 p.m. on the 20th. County Police Team Captures Bandits and Seizes Weapons: Chen Qingxun, the captain of the Second Police Platoon stationed in Luzhuang County, led a team on patrol in the area of Dongxi Yanzhuang and Shangfang Shuidongkou.

According to a secret report, the large bandits from Jiangyin were secretly active in the area. The team immediately apprehended the four members of the bandit army's Red Guard: Mei Bohong (artilleryman), Sun Wanlin (artilleryman), Shen Mingjun (transportation committee member), and Zhang Zhushan (communist party organizing committee member) near Shangfang Shuidongkou. They also seized two Mauser pistols, six homemade cannons, and three bicycles. Issue of Reorganizing County Roads: Nantong County's roads have a total length of over 600 miles. In recent years, they have not been repaired for a long time, and the roadbeds have collapsed and many bridges have become dilapidated. The County Administrative Conference decided that the Construction Bureau should immediately invite the relevant district chiefs to discuss the matter. The County Government specially ordered Director Yao to handle the matter. Local circles expressed great dissatisfaction that the Construction Bureau has as many as fifty employees but has not immediately repaired the county roads.

Changshu 86

Decision to Convert Field Rent at Market Price: This autumn, the conversion of rent payments by tenants in this county was initially determined by the party-government talks to be nine yuan per picul. Later, as the market price suddenly soared, the party-government meeting reduced the price to eight yuan. However, the market price has gradually increased again, and according to the annual custom, the rent price has never been reduced. Therefore, the landlords have repeatedly requested the county government to reconsider. As a result, the county government has not issued a formal announcement, and the landlords' rent collection has also been inconsistent, causing many tenants to wait and see. Yesterday (the 21st), the county administrative conference decided to comply with the instructions of the Provincial Department of Civil Affairs. Since the rent regulations already stipulate that the rent should be converted at the market price, there is no need to add any restrictions. Based on this clause, it was decided to convert the rent at the market price. An official announcement was issued and sent to the County Party Department for reference.

Preparations for County Middle School Games Almost Lead to Tragedy: The county middle school in this county will soon hold its own sports meet. A track was hastily built on the school playground. The school allocated 80 yuan to the physical education instructor, Shen Zhongguang, to purchase cinders and pave the track. The school also borrowed a heavy iron roller from the Construction Bureau to level the track. On the afternoon of the other day, during physical education class, Zhong Jizhong, a boarding student from Mao Village, and others were pushing and pulling the iron roller for fun. Instructor Shen immediately grabbed the iron handle along with student Zhou and ordered more than ten students to push it from behind. As they approached the wall, they needed to retreat. Suddenly, the students in front exerted too much force, and those retreating could not move quickly enough. Zhou Jizhong hesitated slightly and was tripped. The iron roller rolled over Zhou. The iron roller, which was used by the Construction Bureau for building provincial roads, weighed about a thousand pounds. Fortunately, it tilted slightly, so it only injured Zhou's head and buttocks. A hole was torn in his head, and blood flowed non-stop. Someone reported to the principal, Xu Yunyuan, who rushed the student to Jishan Hospital for treatment. The head injury was reported to be more serious than the buttock injury. Fortunately, his life was not in danger. The school games were originally scheduled for the 19th, but after this incident, the school authorities announced that the games would be temporarily suspended and rescheduled.

Jiaxing 87

Former County Public Security Bureau Chief Accused: Judgement in Case Announced: Xu Ajin, a servant at Nanyuan Hall in Jiaxing, was previously forced to serve as a porter by the police, causing his family to starve. After being released by the army upon request, he accused Qiu Zeshen, the current chief of the Second Public Security Precinct, Mo Runxun, the former chief of the County Public Security Bureau, and Fang Zhuangyou, the former secretary of the County Government, of ordering the police to use violence to force people to perform involuntary labor. The High Court designated the Hangzhou Court to hear the case, and the court summoned witnesses for questioning multiple times. Xu Ajin specially hired lawyers Gu Shaoming, Cao Tinglan, Wu Shufang, Chen Dexin, Yu Linquan, and others to represent him pro bono. The debate was concluded a few days ago, and the verdict was announced yesterday. The Hangzhou Court, considering that the defendants were somewhat hasty but not entirely at fault, acquitted them. However, Xu Ajin was very dissatisfied after the hearing and prepared to appeal after receiving the judgment.

Robbery Occurs Outside the North Gate: At around 10 p.m. on the 22nd, a group of six or seven bandits armed with weapons suddenly broke into the home of Shi, a monk, in Shijia Bang, Taiping Bridge, outside Jiaxing's North Gate. They tied up Shi, the monk, and severely beat his son, then looted the place at will. The area is very close to the city. Someone reported the incident to the Third Public Security Precinct, which relayed the information to the military and police agencies. The Second District Department, the Shui Guan County Public Security Bureau, the patrol police brigade, the business association and other armed forces rushed to pursue them, but the bandits had already left without a trace.

Shangyu 88

Ma Jinrong and His Wife Stabbed in Robbery: At night on the 17th, at the home of Ma Jinrong, a farmer in Ma Village, four miles from Yonghe City in the eastern district, a group of bandits armed with sharp knives and sulfur bombs broke down the door and rushed in. Jinrong woke up from a dream and grabbed one of the bandits, shouting for help. The bandit, in a panic, slashed at Jinrong's left arm, nearly severing his left wrist, and then stabbed him several times in the thigh. Jinrong collapsed to the ground, bleeding profusely. His wife, seeing her husband injured, also shouted for help and was stabbed in the left arm. The remaining bandits took the opportunity to loot the house and fled towards the border of Yuyao. The loss of property is estimated at around one or two hundred yuan.

Xiaoshan 89

Already Robbed, Now Hit by Fire: On the night of the 20th, the home of Zhang Jiujin in Zhangjiaban, Xixiang, Xiaoshan County, was filled with guests celebrating a happy event. Suddenly, seven bandits armed with firearms broke in through the door. Three bandits stood guard, and four entered the house to rob. After an hour of looting, they fled eastward. The total loss was more than fifty yuan in cash and clothing and other items worth about 20,000 yuan. Afterwards, a fire broke out in the firewood room. Fortunately, neighbors worked hard to put out the fire and only two flat rooms were destroyed.

Education News Highlights

Ministry of Education Stipulates Distinct Names for Schools 90

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to all provinces and municipalities stipulating the names of schools jointly run by several counties. The original order stated:

It is necessary to clearly distinguish school names based on the source of funding and the nature of the school. However, recent investigations have revealed that in addition to the four types of public schools – National, Provincial, Municipal, and County – there is also a type jointly established by several counties, with funding allocated by several counties or from shared property rentals. This type of school is not solely owned by one county and should not be called "X County Public." To clearly distinguish it, a distinct name should be stipulated in addition to the four types of public school names: National, Provincial, Municipal, and County. It is now stipulated that this distinct name will be "Jointly Established." In the future, all schools jointly established by two locations will be called "XX (abbreviation of the two locations) Jointly Established X School." If the school is jointly established by three or more locations, the first character of the school name can be taken to summarize the locations involved. After this stipulation, all previous names such as "XX United County Public School" or "XX Several County Public X School" should be uniformly corrected.

In addition to issuing separate orders, it is also urgently ordered that each county investigate the schools under its jurisdiction that need to have their names corrected and order them to make the corrections and report them to the Ministry. This is of utmost importance. This order.

The Fourth Plenary Session Approved the Establishment of a Specialized Translation Bureau to Translate

Academic Books from Various Countries 91

At the Fourth Plenary Session, Zhu Jiahua proposed the "Motion to Establish a Specialized Translation Bureau to Translate Academic Books from Various Countries to Popularize New Knowledge to the Nation and to Promote Academic Communication with Various Countries," which was approved in principle and submitted to the National Government for consideration by the Ministry of Education. The original proposal is as follows:

All endeavors are rooted in academics. Academic excellence in other countries is the reason for the revitalization of all aspects. Academic deficiencies in China are the reason why various construction projects are difficult to perfect. Books are the expression of academics and the stepping stones to research. Academic books in other countries are abundant, while in China they are scarce. It is imperative to establish a specialized translation bureau to oversee translation work in order to promote academic research. The positive and negative reasons are outlined below:

China is indeed lacking in research talent, and even those who wish to engage in research have few books to read. There are three reasons for this: (1) They are scattered in various countries and difficult to collect. (2) Different countries have different languages, and those who know one language may not know another. (3) Foreign books are too expensive to purchase easily. Recognizing this, the Japanese made translating Western books their initial approach. Every relatively important book published in the world is immediately translated into Japanese. Not only can it be popularized among the people of their country in writing, but its price is also much cheaper than the original book, which arouses the interest of scholars in their country and encourages them to engage in more in-depth exploration.

Opponents may argue that Japanese translations are mostly done by private individuals on their own initiative and are not entirely controlled by the government. There are now occasional publications of translated books in Chinese bookstores. As long as there is a demand for research, there will naturally be a supply of translations. Why should the government set up a special office to handle this non-urgent matter? This argument seems valid, but it is not. If we look at the newly published materials in bookstores, which are more numerous, academic books or non-academic books? Merchants are profit-oriented and only know how to cater to trends and do not know how to promote trends. Specialized academic books are less needed in China now. They should be actively promoted by the government and should not be allowed to develop naturally. This is precisely what our party aims for: when learning from foreign countries, we must catch up from the beginning and not follow in their footsteps.

Measures: 1. Establish a translation office in the central government and attach a library. In addition to purchasing old famous works from various countries, purchase or exchange new academic publications at any time to ensure that they are collected in detail without any omissions. 2. In addition to being translated by the office itself, professors from domestic universities may be designated to assist in the translation of books to be translated. 3. Private translations may be submitted to the office for review, and high prices may be paid to purchase them to show encouragement. 4. Order provinces and regions to establish libraries universally and purchase books published by the office for public reading in order to promote widespread dissemination. 5. Books published by the office may only charge printing costs in order to keep prices low and make them accessible to the public. 6. The office will regularly review and determine academic terms so that the terms used by translators can be standardized. Are the above-mentioned reasons and measures appropriate? Please make a public decision. Proposer: Zhu Jiahua Co-signer: Chen Lifu

Ministry of Education Stipulates Seals for Overseas Schools 92

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to all consulates abroad stating: Regarding where the seals of overseas Chinese schools should be issued, consuls stationed abroad have repeatedly requested instructions. The Ministry of Education has found that the seals of Chinese schools in places where there are no consulates are temporarily issued by the provincial education departments nearest to the location, and Guangdong Province has been ordered to notify its provincial education department of this matter. In places where consulates have been established, the seals of registered Chinese schools should be issued by the consul and reported to the Ministry for the record in order to ensure uniformity and convenience. In addition to issuing separate orders, the Ministry hereby orders you to be informed and to instruct your subordinate schools to comply. This order is attached with the seal size (5.5 cm on each side).

Liaoning Province's Children's Education Goals 93

Shenyang Correspondence: Wu Jiaxiang, Director of the Department of Education, believes that elementary education is the foundation of the country and the people and is extremely important. Any inadequacies will make it difficult to cultivate healthy and well-rounded citizens. In order to focus on children's education in the province, seven goals for children's training have been stipulated and ordered to be implemented by all elementary schools: (1) A healthy body; (2) Skilled hands for labor; (3) Perfect morals; (4) Noble ideals; (5) A scientific mind; (6) Artistic interests; (7) The spirit of group autonomy.

Shanghai Branch Meeting of the Local Education Research Association 96

The Shanghai Branch of the Jiangsu Provincial Local Education Research Association held its first meeting at the County Education Bureau yesterday. The attendees were Liu Yunshu, Huai Boming, Ma Yiwen, Ding Zezhang, Ji Hongzhang, Zhang Yi, Chen Chen, Wang Panxin, Jin Zuobin, Xu Yunji, Niu Zhiyi, Hu Chaolun, Yang Huiming, Lin Qing, and Zhang Zitao. Under the chairmanship of Director Shi, the association's regulations were approved. The following motions were then discussed: (1) How should the research focus of the association be defined? It was resolved as follows: (1) Continue researching the provisional standards for the syllabus. (2) Matters that were previously discussed by the county branches but did not reach a conclusion. (3) Rural economic survey. (4) Teaching materials for public schools. (2) Should a research period be stipulated for the above issues? It was resolved that the research period should be stipulated as follows: (1) Provisional standards for the syllabus should be concluded by the end of the 19th year. (2) The unresolved matters from the previous county branches should be concluded within this semester. (3) The method of rural economic survey should be concluded within this semester. (4) The teaching materials for public schools should be concluded within the 19th year. (3) How should the research method for the above issues be defined? It was resolved as follows: (1) The syllabus standards should be divided into three groups for research: middle school, elementary school, and kindergarten. The middle school group will be undertaken by the three schools of County Middle School, Sanlin, and Qiangshu. The elementary school group's language will be undertaken by Tangwan Dongming and Yuxiu. Arithmetic will be undertaken by Sanlin, Qiangshu, and Tangwan. Society will be undertaken by Minhang Center, Chenxing, and Beiqiao. Nature will be undertaken by Zhuanqiao, Beiqiao, and Chenxing. Work will be undertaken by Minhang Center, Zhuanqiao, and Guantao. Art will be undertaken by Sanlin and Zhuxi. Music will be undertaken by Minhang Center and Yutang. Physical education will be undertaken by Qiangshu, Yutang, and Yuxiu. The kindergarten group will be undertaken by Chenxing and Sanlin. (2) Zhang Fengshan, Jin Zuobin, and Huai Boming are recommended to draft the method of rural economic survey first and then conduct joint research. (3) The director of this association will send a letter to the various agencies to solicit opinions for the public school teaching materials to be used for practical experimentation in the districts when editing public readings. (4) The date of the next meeting was decided to be 1 p.m. on December 21st. The meeting was adjourned after the discussions.

Lehua Still Lost Yesterday

Lost to Lakers Zero to Two; Better Morale Than Before 104

With Cao Guicheng and Chen Yutian Joining 105

The Lehua soccer team had Cao Guicheng and Chen Yutian joining yesterday, marking a renewal of spirit, completely unlike before. Although the result was a 0-2 loss to Lakers in the Group A match, their actual strength was not far apart.

Cao Guicheng's Reputation Well-Deserved 106

Cao Guicheng of South China is the only right-winger of talent in our country. This time, he came to Shanghai on business and happened to encounter the Lehua vs. Lakers match. He played as an experienced team member to serve the fans in Shanghai. Admiration for his name had been long-standing, and once the news spread, spectators flocked to Shen Garden in numbers rarely seen before. When Li Huitang and Cao Guicheng walked onto the field, the applause was deafening and the welcome was intense, as one can imagine. Mr. Cao lived up to his name. In the intense battle of ninety minutes, he was very effective, almost never failing to make an impact, becoming a dangerous figure among Lehua's forwards. The enemy feared him as if facing a fierce tiger, avoiding his attack. After swapping positions with Chen Yutian, he was also able to handle it with ease. His teammate Chen Yutian was also an outstanding talent. The opportunities created by both were not capitalized upon due to insufficient support from the midfield; otherwise, Lakers' goal would have been hard-pressed to avoid being breached.

Lu Zhong'en Gets His Wish 107

At the beginning of the battle, Cao Guicheng, showing his mettle, was eager to try. The enemy, having heard of his name long ago, feared him like a tiger. Whenever he dribbled forward, they would kick the ball out of bounds, rendering the hero useless. Within five minutes, an opportunity suddenly arose, and Lehua gained a corner kick. Cao kicked powerfully, landing the ball in front of the goal. The goalkeeper caught it but lost it again. With no one else around, it was safely cleared. Then, Lakers' right-winger, Matt, shot at the goal. Lu Zhong'en calmly caught the ball and kicked it to Li Huitang, who passed it again to Chen Yutian. The three passed the ball to Cao Guicheng, who fiercely attacked the goal. Several midfielders crowded in, and goalkeeper Roberts leapt up to punch the ball out, averting the danger for Lakers. But Lehua's danger reappeared, as Lakers took advantage of the internal weakness of Lehua, and five tigers pounced. Lu Zhong'en, seeing the opportunity, decisively left the goal from afar, hoping to turn the tide. A long shot from thirty yards away saved the day, fulfilling his wish.

Simon's Shot Breaks Through 108

Lakers' siege had taken shape. The five forwards either attacked from the left and right flanks or directly from the center, causing Lehua's internal defense to be stretched in all directions, creating a dangerous situation. The second corner kick was safely defended. Subsequently, left-winger Jackson crossed the ball, and center forward Simon lifted his foot, shooting with full force. Lu Zhong'en met the shot with one hand, but could not stop it from rolling into the goal, and the goal was breached. This occurred twenty-five minutes into the game. Cao and Chen made several excellent crosses, but unfortunately, the midfielders on the left were not very effective, making the efforts futile. Li Huitang kicked a free kick, but the goalkeeper caught it. Zhang Baoluo charged and fell to the ground, and no one followed up, resulting in a missed opportunity. In the next ten minutes, Lehua was subjected to even greater pressure. It was a great storm, but fortunately, no danger was encountered. Soon after, Lehua launched a counterattack, with repeated advances being blocked. Chen Yutian penetrated deep into the flank and lifted his right foot, landing the ball right in front of the goal. Yang Renwei headed the ball, but it went high above the goal, causing the audience to sigh in disappointment. In the first half, Lakers led with a score of 1-0.

Li Huitang's Amazing Shot 109

As the second half resumed, Cao Guicheng became very active. Within two minutes, he had passed the foul line and entered the danger zone. The entire Lakers team lost color, behaving coarsely and being penalized for fouls. Li Huitang took the free kick from about twenty-five yards from the goal. He shot directly at the goal, and with a loud bang, the ball missed by only a foot, startling everyone. Lakers reorganized and counterattacked fiercely, probing the goal twice. One attempt was blocked by Lu's body, and the other went high behind the goal. Li Huitang provided strong support, and Chen Yutian rushed forward again on the right. He chipped the ball over inside defender Wu Jianhai, facing an empty goal. Who knew that the handling would be improper, turning all hope into smoke.

Tommy Gets It Without Effort 110

Lehua's main player, Li Huitang, realizing that the attack force of the forwards was uneven on the left and right, changed the formation, personally taking the central forward position, while Wu Jianhai was moved to left midfielder, and Wang Jihua was reassigned to central defender. The forwards subsequently made several amazing moves. However, the opportunities for counterattack were minimal, and the internal defense was chaotic due to the loss of a pillar. Half of the team's territory was ravaged by others. Fortunately, Lakers' shooting technique was poor; otherwise, even with Lu's good defense, Lehua could not have guaranteed avoiding trouble. In the final five minutes, Lakers' Matt chipped the ball to the center. Wang Shusen kicked the ball against the goalpost, and it bounced back in front of Tommy, who headed it into the net. Lehua redoubled its efforts, hoping to recover a goal or two, but the situation was irreversible, and time was running out. As a result, Lehua lost to Lakers 0-2. The referee was Jiang Xiangqing.

Results of Yesterday's Chinese Football Association Matches 114

Zhenru won against Qingnian (Middle Group): 5-1

Zhendan drew with Shita (Middle Group): 0-0

Zhendan won against British-American (Football Group): 4-3

The women's basketball team of Liangjiang Women's Physical Education School triumphantly returned to Shanghai from Tianjin yesterday. (Photo by Wang Kai)

Zhenru won against Qingnian (Middle Group). The Zhenru team is very strong and has high hopes of winning the Middle Group championship. However, the Qingnian team is also a rising force, formed by players from both Fudan and Shanghai-Jiangnan Universities. Players like Hu Minteng, Qu Hongde, and Yu Shunzhang are quite well-known. Yesterday afternoon at 3 PM, the two teams faced off at the Chinese baseball field, with He Chunhui as the referee. Qingnian's momentum was extremely strong, invading Zhenru's area, charging left and right, with sharp offense. Right-winger Zhu Xiaorong's passing was effective, and left-winger Yao Yongbing relayed from the middle to right forward Zhou Shaowen, who lifted his foot and scored, opening the scoring. Zhenru quickly counterattacked, questioning the opponent, and a dangerous situation formed in front of Qingnian's goal. Zhenru's center forward, Luo Haixian, got the ball and scored, and the momentum grew stronger. After a few minutes, Zhenru's Luo Haixian scored a second time, making the score 2-1 in Zhenru's favor in the first half. At the start of the second half, Qingnian tried to retaliate, but Zhenru also showed no weakness. After a short stalemate, Zhenru suddenly became courageous, surrounding Qingnian's goal. Qingnian's defender, Qu Hongde, became the target of attack, struggling to cope. Fortunately, he was agile and able to defuse the danger. Qingnian then launched an invasion, but Zhenru was well-prepared and impenetrable. After more than twenty minutes, Zhenru's left forward, Cai Rongrui, on the left wing, sent a long ball in front of Qingnian's goal, unexpectedly breaking through and scoring, causing the spectators to laugh. In the next ten or so minutes, Zhenru's Luo Haixian scored two more goals. Qingnian's disorganized defense failed to achieve anything. As a result, Zhenru won 5-1.

Zhendan drew with Baota (Middle Group). The Zhendan team consists not only of Chinese players but also several Western players. The team fought Baota yesterday at the track and field, and the two teams were evenly matched and difficult to separate. After an intense battle, neither side scored. The referee was Tang Zhongguang.

Chairman Chiang's Trip to Jiangxi 124

Will Depart from Nanjing at the End of This Month

Will Stay for Two Weeks and Then Return to Nanjing

Vice-Commander Zhang Also Scheduled to Go North at the End of the Month

Songhu Garrison Commander Xiong Shihui went to Nanjing to meet with Chairman Chiang to discuss important official matters. He returned to Shanghai only the morning before yesterday. As reported yesterday, reporters visited him and learned that Chairman Chiang's trip to Jiangxi to suppress the bandits is expected to take place at the end of this month. He is scheduled to stay for two weeks and then return to Nanjing to handle affairs. Vice-Commander Zhang is also unable to leave Nanjing for the time being because the issue of incorporating the remnants of Yan and Feng's forces still needs to be thoroughly discussed with Chairman Chiang. Therefore, his trip north is also expected to be around the end of the month.

National Calendar Settlement Issues

Various Industries Request Assistance from the Financial Sector 125

Settling accounts at the end of the National Calendar year is inevitable. However, various industries such as soybean, rice, and native products are facing difficulties in collecting debts due to the inability of debtors to repay. Meanwhile, debts owed to the financial sector must be repaid in accordance with government orders. Furthermore, in order to meet sales targets and social demand, more goods must be prepared outside of the National Calendar year. As such, working capital is inevitably strained. Therefore, many advocate requesting that banks and money shops, after the settlement of accounts at the end of the National Calendar year, allow repayment of current accounts but also provide additional short-term loans (i.e., one or two months) for turnover. It is reported that the money shops find this request reasonable and may consider it.

Negotiations to Recover the French Concession Tribunal

The Foreign Ministry and the French Ambassador Will Conduct Negotiations 126

Regarding the issue of recovering the French Concession Tribunal, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is preparing to begin negotiations with the French Ambassador, Mr. Wilden. Foreign Minister Wang Zhengting stated to people in Shanghai yesterday that the French Ambassador has been staying in Nanjing to discuss matters since presenting his credentials and has not returned to Shanghai. Upon his return to Nanjing this time, his first step will be to negotiate with him on the recovery of the French Concession Tribunal, and after making some progress, he will proceed with other negotiations.

Central Temporary Bondholders' Association

Appeals for Assistance from the Financial Sector 127

Yesterday, Letters Were Sent Out

Requesting Assistance

The Central Bank Temporary Exchange Bondholders' Association sent letters yesterday to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Bankers' Association, the Money Shops Association, the National Chamber of Commerce Federation, the Chambers of Commerce of various provinces, cities, and counties, and various organizations, requesting their unanimous sympathy and assistance. The letter stated: "To all whom it may concern, the General Headquarters of the National Revolutionary Army, with the approval of the National Government on August 26 of the 15th year of the Republic of China, entrusted the Political Affairs Bureau and the Treasury of the General Headquarters to issue Central Bank Temporary Exchange Bonds worth 5 million yuan in silver dollars. The bonds were divided into denominations of 1 yuan, 5 yuan, and 10 yuan, and were stamped with the seal of the General Headquarters of the National Revolutionary Army and the official seals of the Director of the Political Affairs Bureau and the Treasurer. The General Headquarters formulated regulations and promulgated them, instructing that they be fully accepted and used. These exchange bonds once circulated in Shanghai, but were suddenly suspended from redemption, causing significant losses to merchants and civilians. Today, four years have passed, and merchants and civilians have repeatedly appealed to the government to recover and redeem them, but no appropriate solution has been found. The issuance of these exchange bonds was originally intended to subsidize the Northern Expedition, which was beneficial to the military affairs of the Northern Expedition. The National Government should recover and redeem them as soon as possible to alleviate the people's difficulties. Now that the military affairs have ended and the country is unified, the central government is striving to govern with diligence and renewing the country with the people. Domestic and foreign public debts are being consolidated as a whole, the country's prestige is increasing day by day, and the people's recovery is expected. The significance of the Central Bank Temporary Exchange Bonds is as important as stated above, and its nature is absolutely different from other domestic debts and cannot be compared with them. Therefore, the government must recover and redeem them in full as soon as possible. In addition to petitioning the National Government and Chairman Chiang to instruct the Ministry of Finance to redeem them immediately to alleviate the people's hardships, we have always admired your association's leadership of the business community and its role as the financial hub. We dare to send this special letter and humbly request that you show your sympathy and assistance. This will not only be fortunate for the members of our association but also a blessing for commerce and people's livelihoods. With urgent words, we cannot express our gratitude enough."

Petition to the Ministry of Finance to Recover National Treasury Bonds

Telegram to the Central Government 128

The National Treasury Bondholders' Association of the Ministry of Finance of the National Government sent a petition yesterday to the National Government, the Executive Yuan, and the Ministry of Finance, stating: "The Ministry of Finance, in order to subsidize the national treasury and regulate finance, issued National Treasury Bonds worth 9 million yuan on June 30 of the 16th year of the Republic of China. The bonds were divided into denominations of 1 yuan, 5 yuan, and 10 yuan, with an annual interest rate of 6%. The Ministry of Finance formulated regulations and ordered their promulgation, issuing them in three installments over three months, with 3 million yuan issued each month. The bonds were to be redeemed by the national treasury six months after the date of issuance, and the bonds were marked with the words 'can be redeemed at the Central Bank of each province upon maturity.' These treasury bonds were fully issued and circulated, but time has passed, and they are now overdue by three years. Merchants and civilians holding the bonds have received neither principal nor interest, which has had a severe impact on people's livelihoods. Now that the situation is stable and the country is unified, the Ministry of Finance should promptly reorganize these national treasury bonds and order the Central Bank of each province to redeem them immediately to uphold government orders and maintain credibility. We humbly submit this petition and hope that you will consider and implement it, for the benefit of both the public and the people."
