Free Talk

Laugh It Off 191

— Sea Traveler

A: Your child is how old this year? He is really naughty.

B: He is five years old this year, but he is very naughty and doesn't listen to his parents.

A: Children are mostly like that.

B: No, he was always well-behaved, but after winning a "handsome face" award in a children's competition three months ago, he became arrogant and showed disobedience to us.

—Mr. C is a bachelor and has always been very happy, but recently he has been frowning and sighing to people.

B: Maybe there has been some bereavement in his family.

A: No, it's just because he recently got engaged.

A's Wife: My husband is the most frugal person in the world.

B's Wife: How is he frugal? Please tell me so I can teach my husband when I get home.

A's Wife: When he writes a letter and sticks on a stamp, he only puts a little saliva on the four corners and refuses to completely wet it to avoid wasting the saliva in his mouth.

A: I heard that you went to the north to get married this time and returned south how proud.

B: What's so proud? It just added to the burden.

A: I heard that your father-in-law has quite a bit of money. Did he give you anything?

B: Yes, he simply gave me the whole family. Old and young all live in my small family.

Travel Notes of Rongjiang 192

— Yì Nóng

I came from Fujian to Zhejiang, passing through the Ao River, crossing the Feiyun Ferry, and arriving at the Ou River, also known as the Rong River. It is named Rong River because the mountains and waters of Yongjia are beautiful and the residences are elegant. Every family has a small garden planted with hibiscus. Around the Double Ninth Festival, when the flowers bloom, they are white in the morning, pink at noon, and red in the evening, changing color three times in one day, hence the name "Three Drunkennesses." Although it is not as prosperous as it used to be, there are still tall hibiscus plants towering above the clouds in people's fences and ancient temples. The abundance of flowers and the beauty of the colors are the most brilliant scenery in the autumn. Xie Kang Le said, "The hibiscus in the early sun," he must have seen something and said that. This is the origin of the name Rong River. In the river, the solitary island is charming, and the twin pagodas compete for beauty. There is a temple in the middle called Jiangxin Temple. Monk Dixian once presided over this temple. Above is Haoran Tower and Chengxian Pavilion. Next to it is the Wen Tianxiang Shrine. The couplets on the pillars and the inscriptions on the walls are beautiful beyond words. The hermit of Taihe Mountain has a couplet that says, "Floating clouds and solitary islands change with the tide, and the barren tombs in the evening rain enter the cold dream." This is a realistic record. To the east of the river, adjacent to the city, there is Feixia Cave, where Liu Gen of the Song Dynasty cultivated himself. Above is the Woshu Tower. Below the tower is a camphor tree that can be embraced. It protrudes diagonally through the window, and its winding shape is like a sleeping tree, hence the name Woshu Tower. Climbing this tower, one can see the overlapping green mountains in the distance and the green fields in the vicinity. With nearby water and distant mountains, there are endless poetic thoughts. At the foot of the mountain is Xie Gongyan, which used to be a place for Xie Gong to relax. The Taoists in the cave planted peaches for their own enjoyment. The tour paths are winding and graceful, although it is not a paradise outside the world. However, a few years ago, due to carelessness, the fire burned the tower and scorched the trees, and now it is half withered. Thinking of the past and the present, one cannot help but sigh. To the south of the river is Huagai Mountain, with Daguan Pavilion, Jigu Pavilion, and Zifu Temple on it. They were all famous scenic spots in the past. Today, a wide road has been opened to build Zhongshan Park. Leaning against the mountains and surrounded by water, the scenery is beautiful. Gentlemen and ladies stroll around, their hairpins and clothes fragrant, chatting and drinking tea to relieve their mood. The construction of the park was planned by the poet Zheng Jiangmen, and it has become a magnificent sight. At the foot of the mountain is Huangye Village, where there is a Ou Society, a place where poets and lyricists gather to recite poems and compose verses, created by the lyric master Lin Tiezun. Today, friends are scattered, and the sound of chanting is silent. To the west of the river, adjacent to the city, there is Yifeng Pavilion. Although this pavilion is only a few bows wide, its architecture is exquisite. Overlooking the river and admiring the mountains, its scenery is particularly charming. The sails and sand crows fluttering between the distant shores of the setting sun are like painting a natural picture. Recently, the autumn sky is clear and the water and trees are bright, and all things are quiet and secluded. Friends in Ou led me to Yangyuan to admire the chrysanthemums. The owner of the garden is Yang Yuanfeng and Danfeng, two hermits who live a simple life and use growing chrysanthemums as their livelihood. They carefully study irrigation and cultivation methods for decades. When the flowers bloom, they invite friends to recite poems and drink wine to appreciate them. Their colors are clear and beautiful, their fragrance is secluded and far-reaching, and their varieties are unique and elegant. Not only does Ou Zhong have no such good varieties, but there are also varieties that chrysanthemum artists in Shanghai have never seen. Yangyuan is the best place for chrysanthemums in Ou Zhong. The poems and verses of singing and harmonizing have filled the chest. I said that the Yang brothers' happiness cannot be exchanged even for a king facing south. As for the accumulated green of Songtai, the clarity and openness of Jiushan, and the pleasant garden of the Zeng family and the Yu garden of the Lü family, although each has its own pleasing scenery, I was unable to visit them all one by one due to busy matters, and I still feel nostalgic in my heart. Only by paddling a small boat and touring the Hualiu Pond and the Qianhu area did I see the hibiscus on the shore still reflecting in the setting sun. The splendor of the scenery is different from that of the early sun, with a rich and beautiful appearance that makes people forget their fatigue when they see it. Returning home, I had nothing to do, so I moistened my brush and wrote a record of it. I have three poems to record its victory, which are attached below: The scenery of Rongjiang is naturally quiet and secluded, and the heavens give poets free rein. The autumn colors fill the river, and the early sun is beautiful. The tourist has been famous for thousands of years. The happiness of growing chrysanthemums in Yangyuan is a natural pleasure. The cold beauty and secluded fragrance remind me of the righteous and famous scholars of the Jin Dynasty. The poet's feelings and the hero's wine are used to appreciate the flowers every year. The guest's home is at the end of the Cang River. Every time the flowers bloom, I still love the flowers. After parting, my feelings are melancholy. Looking at the Yingying autumn water, I hope for Jianjia.

Storms in the Sea of Love 193

— Thin Gull

Recently, there have been rumors outside that the photographer Mr. Lin Xuehuai and the movie star Ms. Hu Die have broken up. Most of the words are speculation and cannot be believed. Gull and both parties are old friends and know the details quite well. I dare to give readers a truthful report.

Xuehuai has recently made a lot of profit in the gold business. However, people in the gold business often like to gamble, so Xuehuai also indulged a little. Miss Die knew about it and was not happy. Xuehuai was also a little concerned that Miss Die often liked to go out at night. Last Sunday, they had a verbal conflict. This is just a normal state of children and there is no so-called breakup. Currently, friends are acting as Lu Zhonglian, hoping to clear the clouds and see the moon again.

Rare News from the Theatrical World 194

— Master of the Plum Blossom Pavilion

Mei Lanfang and Yang Xiaolou to Arrive in Shanghai Simultaneously

Rumors of Mei Wan-hua [Mei Lanfang], owner of the Zhui Yu Xuan studio, coming to Shanghai have been circulating for a long time. Now, we have received confirmation. We are delighted to hear that Mr. Mei is expected to arrive in Shanghai around the 25th of this month, and no later than the 27th. This is because the 28th is the 70th birthday celebration of the mother of Chairman Chen Tiaoyuan. It is rare for a person to live to seventy years old, and his colleagues have specially initiated a grand theatrical performance to celebrate Madam's birthday. A month ago, Mr. Chen had already sent someone to Peiping to invite Mei to Shanghai to perform on stage as scheduled. Wan-hua originally had plans to visit Shanghai, so he happily agreed. The reason why he must arrive by the 27th is because there was an early agreement with the Chen residence that could not be changed.

The Chen residence originally intended to invite the three giants, Mei (Lanfang), Yang (Xiaolou), and Yu (Shuyan), for the theatrical performance. However, when the representative of the Chen residence arrived in Peiping, Little Yu was weak and ill and firmly refused to risk the trip. Although efforts were made to persuade him through various connections, the result was still negative. After Yang Xiaolou returned to Peiping from Lotus Mountain, he was in good spirits. Upon introduction by someone, a deal was made for 18,000 yuan. However, during the negotiations, Xiaolou made two conditions: (1) The performance period was set for three days, and no additional days could be added temporarily. He must return to Peiping after singing for three days. (2) He would not perform in any charity performances. The Chen residence should provide a firm guarantee that if there were any difficulties, the Chen residence would be responsible for handling them and politely decline any refusals. The representative of the Chen residence fully agreed to both requirements, and the agreement was concluded. This is a rough account of Xiaolou's arrival in Shanghai. It is also rumored that Xiaolou's arrival in Shanghai will be around the same time as Wan-hua's.

Kun actress Xue Yanqin performed at the Tiansheng Stage for more than a month and gained a great reputation. Her performance period has expired and she took a boat north on the 20th.

Kun actress Du Liyun's reputation rose sharply after going to Peiping the year before last. Under the careful guidance of Wang Yaoqing, her art has also improved day by day. She is currently performing in rotation at the Kai Ming Theater and Harbin Film Theater in the old capital, and both are sold out every day. It is now heard that a theater in Shanghai has sent people to Peiping to repeatedly invite Du, but Du has repeatedly declined with humility, and it is expected that she will come to Shanghai next autumn.

Musical Notes: The Pingsheng Music Society of this city has been promoting Kunqu opera for 20 years. In addition to regular monthly meetings, they also hold joint performances. The third joint performance this month will be held at the Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association at 1 p.m. on the 23rd. All the supporting roles are members of the society, which is not easy. The program for the day is as follows:

Daytime Performances: (The Story of the Pipa) Appreciating the Lotus, Cutting Hair, Selling Hair, Sweeping Pine; (Romance of the Western Chamber) Visiting the Temple, Making a Racket, Sending a Letter, A Good Time; (Lu Lin); (Legend of the White Snake) Burning Incense, Water Duel, Broken Bridge, Reunion.

Evening Performances: (The Peony Pavilion) Encouraging Agriculture, School, Strolling in the Garden and Praising Flowers, Piling Flowers, A Startling Dream, Searching for a Dream, Flower Judge; (Mistakes of the Kite) A Startling Ugly Face, First Relatives, Later Relatives, Tea Gathering.

News from the Publishing World: The novel "Miss Xue Ping" by Huo Xueming has been published by Jinwu Bookstore. It extensively explores the topic of love and expresses his personal views. Mr. Huo has also recently published "Understanding Love," a collection of essays priced at 25 cents, and "Goose," a collection of short stories priced at 35 cents. Both can be ordered by mail from the Shanghai Xiaodongmen Hunan Correspondence Society without postage.

Acknowledgments and Introductions: Mr. Wei Juezhong, who plans to travel the world by bicycle, has traveled all over Southeast Asia. Recently, he published a book in Shanghai called "Southern Wilderness Peoples," which is sold by the Oriental Bookstore at 306 Nanjing Road, Shanghai, and the Beijiao Bookstore at 32 Sandeli, Baoshan Road. The book records very strange things, but they are indeed the author's personal experiences and notes taken at any time. We received a complimentary copy yesterday and would like to express our gratitude and introduce it.

Travelogue of Southeast Asia (81) 195

— Linghua

Returning with Daoist to Lin Baohua's place at the Oriental Printing Company in Chinatown to visit Master Wan Hui. Master Wan is the younger brother of the literary figure Xie Wu-liang. He studied in India for twelve years, learned Sanskrit, and now teaches Chinese at Yangon University. He is proficient in English and Sanskrit and became a monk early on, using science and literature to connect Buddhist Zen. Many Westerners admire and learn from him. In the afternoon, Master Wan came to Lin's place, and his discussion of his learning was very profound and difficult to understand at once. He is truly a rare gem among Eastern scholars and deserves the respect of humans and gods. Master Wan said that Buddhist studies are in meditation, not like the empty talk of the Middle Kingdom. He studies English and Sanskrit to compare world languages and wants to create a new character that integrates Eastern and Western civilizations. If the country and society are strong, should they not help this great talent to accomplish an immortal career?

On the 28th, I woke up in the morning and saw many yellow-robed young monks walking around the street, holding alms bowls in their right hands. Many of them had beautiful faces. Occasionally, there were elderly monks, and I almost thought that Ananda and Kashyapa were everywhere. I got a poem:

Yellow robes come and go, Ananda is seen, holding an alms bowl and begging for a cold meal from door to door. Overthrowing the country is truly a strong man. Who says that dragons and elephants have withered?

Myanmar monks differ from Chinese monks in many ways. First, Myanmar monks are masculine and promote revolution. Their leader is U. Ottama, who traveled to Japan and recently returned due to illness. It is a pity that after he passed through Xiamen, no Chinese knew to contact him. There are 100,000 Myanmar monks, and it is said that there are many in the old capital of Mandalay. There are monks holding knives and sticks in front of the masses, and the British are also afraid of them.

On the 29th, there was a blind monk who said he had walked from Yunnan and was from Hubei. The blind man had no money and traveled thousands of miles but could not return home. However, it is strange that he was able to come. Chinese monks also wear yellow robes in Myanmar, but the Burmese do not respect them very much because they know that their precepts are not as good as Myanmar monks. And Chinese monks sometimes do very unseemly things. There is a Gao Wanbang here who is very respectful of monks. When a certain monk came, Gao put in a lot of effort to raise a lot of money, getting 5,000 yuan. Later, the monk married a Burmese woman and still did not leave. Gao was very embarrassed and regretted it. From then on, even if the monks were adulterous, he would not treat them politely. The Daoist said that the reason for their marriage was because the Burmese had a custom of touching their feet with their hands. However, it is said that the behavior of Myanmar monks, though said to be perfect, is only because the Burmese are devout in their belief in monks, even if they have it, they do not say it and do not change their belief. Master Wan said that Myanmar monks are clean and noble and rarely commit adultery, able to adhere to the rules left by Sakyamuni. If you go to a Myanmar monastery, it is common to see women there, but you should not suspect them of having other relationships, as they are often their family members. The reason why Burmese Buddhism has maintained the faith of its people to this day is because the monks can keep the precepts.

Warmth in the Heart (320) 196

— Bao Tianxiao

Episode 15: Tears Stream Down in All Directions, Red Feelings of Sorrow; Hearts Open in One Place, Lingering Green Thoughts

The word "fate" in Buddhism is truly an unbreakable term. Whether it is a good fate or a bad fate, once it gets a hold of you, it is difficult to break free. Even the smallest thing has a fate within it. As the saying goes, "Those who are destined will meet across a thousand miles, while those who are not destined will not meet face to face." Zuo Shichen and Green Thoughts seem to have a little bit of fate. Even he himself does not understand where this fate comes from. Is it because Green Thoughts is like Ruiyun, and he appreciates Green Thoughts in memory of Ruiyun? But after becoming familiar with Green Thoughts, he felt that Green Thoughts was Green Thoughts and definitely not Ruiyun. Did he get a new interest and new love for Green Thoughts? But there are also more beautiful singing girls than Green Thoughts. Why does Zuo Shichen have a little bit of concern in his heart only for this little girl? Isn't this about the word "fate"? Moreover, later on, he gradually discovered that Green Thoughts had two quirks in her demeanor. One quirk was that she often used the tip of her tongue to lick her cherry lips. At least two or three times in every mirror scene. Zuo Shichen asked her why she did this. Was it because her lips were dry, so she used that fragrant saliva to moisten them? She said that she didn't even notice that it had become a habit of nature. But she also knew that she had this quirk and couldn't change it for a while. She hated herself deeply. According to her mother, she had been like this since she was a child. Sometimes, she would pinch the tip of her tongue because of this quirk, but she could never change it. A friend said that Green Thoughts's previous life must have been as snake reincarnated. When asked what the basis for this was, he said that he had once heard a famous storyteller named Wu Xigeng say in a book called "The Legend of the White Snake" that the white snake spirit transformed into a peerless beauty and came to repay her gratitude. The storyteller, famous for his subtlety, described the demeanor of the peerless beauty, the White Maiden, as also saying that her clove-like tongue sometimes stretched outwards. He also said that this was a kind of original appearance of a snake. Isn't a snake's tongue frequently stretched outwards? Based on that kind of nonsense, that friend also said that Green Thoughts was a snake reincarnated. That was originally a joke, but Zuo Shichen's heart was clouded, but he didn't say that she was ugly. Instead, he felt that it increased her charm. He argued that there are three things in the world that hate mediocrity the most: one is landscape, the second is writing, and the third is beauty. You want a thousand cliffs and ravines, flying waterfalls and dangerous cliffs, to show the world's majesty. If it is flat, wouldn't it be better for nature to create this world without mountains and water, just a flat plain? As for writing, it is the same. If you give it a comment saying that it is flat and flawless, then there is no need to write this article to waste ink. The ancient saying "Writing is like looking at mountains, it does not like flatness" cannot be said to be meaningless. As for beauty, he also has an argument.

Commercial News

Precious Metals Market Spiked Last Week 197

The trend of the precious metals market last week was sharp, but with many changes. It was difficult to grasp the situation due to confusing and uncertain news, which made people feel alienated. The fluctuations were between three or four taels or six or seven taels per day. As for the rest of the market and exchange rates, there was a slight rotation. On Monday (November 17th), the large silver bars continued to rise, so the spot price for the current month was slightly lower, opening at 77.5 taels. After that, it fluctuated by more than one tael. In the afternoon, it was suddenly reported that Hamaguchi's injuries were critical, and Yuanxing, Yongyuan, Chengyong, Hongli, and others dumped their holdings, causing a sudden drop to 76.5 taels. As a result, it rebounded by one tael and closed at 77.6 qian, slightly lower than last Saturday. On this day, the fluctuation was only around three taels, and the exchange rate was still stable. The next day, the silver market contracted, and the exchange rate was reduced by half a point. The internal market was also strong, with Chinese merchants buying, so the precious metals market stepped onto the blue clouds and suddenly broke through the 80-tael mark. The opening was 80.08 taels. It was said that the United States was inclined to buy silver bars, and it was also heard that Hamaguchi was fine, especially Hengxing and Shengda, who traded heavily. Around noon, it rose to more than 85 taels. Cuita, Jiutai, Fuxingyong, Yuda, Yongfeng, and others came to buy. In the afternoon, it was also heard that banks in the United States had collapsed to prevent large silver bars from falling, and the exchange rate in Mumbai repeatedly reported small amounts. Therefore, the major players in the market competed to buy, and it actually rose to 87 taels. The difference between the high and low prices of the market was more than six taels. On Wednesday, the silver market continued to fall, and the exchange rate was reduced by half a point. Chenfengyong, Yongfeng, Wupin, and others competed to buy, causing a sudden surge to 90.2 qian during the expansion. The Indian conference was feared to raise the silver market, and Xieyu, Fuchang, Lichang, and others successively dumped their holdings, and then immediately broke through the 90-tael mark. In the afternoon, the other party was still mostly only 83.4 taels. The closing price was 84.2 qian, which was a reaction against the trend of the previous day, falling by 2.7 qian. On this day, the difference between the high and low prices was nearly 7 taels. The situation was almost one of a clear tightening and a hidden loosening, and the drifting of the market conditions was really difficult to guess. The next day, the market conditions changed slightly by three or four taels. In the morning, the market was still stable due to the rise in large silver bars, and the opening price was still at 84 taels, but then it went down by two taels due to Xinxing selling. Afterwards, rumors spread that the Sino-American loan had failed, and the market was boosted, rising sharply to 86 taels. However, Fuchang, Yuanheng, and others came out again to sell, and Hengxingshengda also had sales, so the closing price was within 84 taels, down 3 qian from the previous day. Although the Xianling listed price was up by half a point, the difference between the clear and hidden prices was vast. Chinese merchants still had buying, so the internal market seemed strong. The next day, the large silver bars rose again, and Xianling did not change. However, the internal market was slightly tight, and each gold shop continued to buy without stopping. Therefore, the precious metals market had rebounded by more than two taels. The major players all entered from 84 taels in the morning to 88.5 taels in the evening. However, in the end, Yuanxingyong, Fuchang, and others competed to sell, and in an instant, it fell by more than two taels to close at 6.1 qian, which was still up 2.2 qian from the previous day. On Saturday, the large silver bars rebounded, and Xianling shrank by half a point. The internal market was also strong, and the precious metals market rose early due to the United States' inclination to sell copper coins. The market was high, and then rose to 88.9 qian. There were many buyers. Xieyu and Yuanheng then sold, and it fell by two taels. Afterwards, the price rose and fell between 87 and 88 taels. By noon, it was 89 taels, and the closing price was 89 qian, which was up 2.8 qian from the previous day. The difference between the high and low prices in half a day was 2.1 qian. The market atmosphere was still favorable. However, the transactions of each shop were very different. The Cause and Effect of High Interest Rates and Low Yangli 200

Yesterday, the silver interest rate suddenly tightened, which attracted the attention of various businesses. Here is what I have heard. The reason for the loose silver in the past was due to the National Lunar Year closing issues and watching. Now, it is heard that the industries are generally consistent in ending the National Year, and Qianzhuang expresses sympathy to it. At present, they can engage in collecting arrears, and those who lack a share will inevitably be requested. In addition, yesterday was Sunday, and the banks closed, and the lining could not circulate, resulting in this result. As for the fall in Yangli, it was purely due to stagnant digestion and pressure from the tight silver. The banks did not dare to buy more, and there was no news of the foreign line going to the stomach. A reactionary impression suddenly arose in the market, and the result was a fall of thousands of miles, becoming yesterday's decline.

The Securities Market: The Bond Market Was Booming Last Week 201

The prices were firm and strong…Transactions totaled more than 63 million yuan

The bond market in this city last week saw a slight increase in spot transactions compared to the previous period, but trading was still sparse. The total turnover for the week was 132,500 yuan, including 45,500 yuan for reorganized and demobilized soldiers, 12,000 yuan for finance, 29,000 yuan for the 19 Customs, 10,000 yuan for the 96 bonds, and only a few thousand yuan for other bonds. Futures were better than the previous week, and daily transactions were quite active. The first day of the week reached more than 16.4 million yuan, and the next two days were around 1 to 2 million yuan. On Thursday, it was also more than 9.1 million yuan, and on the last two days of the weekend, it was about 7 million yuan each. The total turnover for the week was 62,825,000 yuan, which was more than 9 million yuan more than the previous week. The 9-year Customs was similar to the previous week, totaling 5,565,000 yuan for November and 10,099,000 yuan for December. The 96 reorganized and demobilized soldiers were more active than the previous week, totaling 4,440,000 yuan for November and 10,515,000 yuan for November. The reorganized and demobilized soldiers totaled 3,950,000 yuan for November and 8,060,000 yuan for December. The reorganized soldiers totaled 3,965,000 yuan for November and 7,970,000 yuan for December. However, other bonds remained quiet. The whole 6 Aftermath 19-volume and other bonds were clearer than before. The whole 6 bonds totaled 730,000 yuan for November and 1,770,000 yuan for December. The 19-year cigarette bond totaled 655,000 yuan for November and 495,000 yuan for December. The Customs bond totaled 1,420,000 yuan for November and 2,430,000 yuan for December. The Aftermath bond totaled 410,000 yuan for November and 25,000 yuan for December. The Financial bond totaled 100,000 yuan for November and 260,000 yuan for December. The 7-year 50,000 yuan bond and the continued 2 and 5 were calculated at 10,000 yuan. There was no market for the continued volume. The market situation of each bond in December was much more active than in November because the futures transactions in November were approaching settlement, and each was engaged in swap settlement. In the past week, the price trend of each bond was very good due to the increasing stability of the current situation and the reorganization of domestic and foreign debts, which was welcomed by general investors in government bonds. Therefore, the bond market environment was very good, so the price continued to rise compared to the previous period. As a result, only the reorganized and demobilized soldiers, 96 finance, and Aftermath bonds were only a few jiao higher than the previous week, and the 19-volume bonds were higher than before. The 19-volume and reorganized and demobilized bonds were the most in demand, continuing to rise by 2 to 3 yuan, and the Customs and whole 6 bonds rose by 1 yuan. The current price of the 96 and 19-year Customs government bonds has exceeded 6 yuan. The situation in the bond market is very good. Cotton Yarn Market Weaker After Initial Strength Last Week 202

The cotton yarn market was still strong at the beginning of the week because raw cotton had a squeeze on the near month. The Yunnan gang was more active, which boosted morale. However, the actual demand was not sustainable, and each gang was lifeless. Moreover, the bottom goods inevitably increased. The five blessings and shepherd cotton yarn were particularly heavily stocked, and the trend became more sluggish. Therefore, the other party's attitude was calm, and in fact, the overall situation was more pessimistic. Because of this, people's hearts were scattered. Midway through the week, a certain manufacturer adopted a negative attitude and successively sold off the long positions. The market plate was even more loose. The trading on the floor was also deserted throughout the week. The demand for current cotton yarn was bleak. If the spot sales could not be sustained for a long time, the future would still be difficult to secure.

The Near Month of Hankou Standard Cotton Tended to Be Squeezed Last Week 203

At the beginning of the week, the cotton market saw too many November transactions, and the retail investors were short, anticipating that there would be insufficient delivery, so the buying side had the idea of squeezing the near month. Therefore, the near month was tight and not released, and the far month was agitated. This month, the far month has seen as high as 32 taels and 2 and a half qian, but in fact, there has been no improvement. Therefore, Japanese merchants sold off. Not long after, the US financial sector experienced a major panic, and the US cotton fell slightly. The atmosphere suddenly became vacant, and the market suddenly fell by 5 or 6 qian. However, the Ningbo gang and the Shanghai gang were still reluctant to let go of their purchases due to the harassment of Hankou Road by bandits, which made the source still scarce. However, in terms of the world situation, Indian cotton is cheap, and Chinese and foreign factories have large orders for days. Chinese cotton transactions have completely occupied it, and future changes may not be small. US cotton fell by 25 pounds compared to last week, it is said.

Foreign Cotton Market Slightly Recovered 204

Yesterday, the American cotton market was firm. Initially, it was firm due to short covering, and later due to profit-taking by some longs. Futures prices fluctuated by one to five points. Spot prices for American cotton remained unchanged. English cotton futures rose by two points, while spot prices fell by two points. Spot prices for Egyptian cotton remained unchanged. The Indian cotton market saw Japanese merchants buying both near and far-term Pingguoer futures. Bai Luo and Han futures both fell by one point. Grain and Rice Market Indeed Turned Higher 205

Zhabei: Yesterday, the supply from the inland gradually decreased because the continuous sharp decline in this port had caused significant losses to traders, leading them to adopt a wait-and-see attitude. The producing market initially followed the situation in Shanghai, but the downstream market then turned firm due to inquiries from merchants. The number of rice boats heading to Shanghai decreased. However, at the start of the morning market, the shops in this street were eager, and the new japonica market became active. Prices rose sharply by ten cents. The price of Zhongguan rice had to rise by as much as forty cents. Special top-grade japonica rice rose to about fifteen yuan and thirty cents. Unfortunately, such goods were very scarce in the market. The Bo Tao market was slightly tight. The Yang Xian followed the japonica market, rising by twenty cents. Du Jian rose by one and a half to two and a half cents. The price increase was extremely loose because after frequent fatigue, once the trend improved, the reaction was bound to be intense. The supply of good-quality rice in this port was scarce and stable. Special high-quality rice opened at about twelve yuan and sold well. Chang Jin and Dao Yuan rice both reached fifteen yuan.

South Shanghai: Yesterday, the supply from the river area started sluggish, then became active. Chang Bang white rice initially continued the momentum from the previous day, and selling was very strong. Prices showed a downward trend. Later, upon receiving news from the north that prices were rising, the situation became active. However, the market had already fluctuated by one or two cents. Special top-grade high-quality japonica rice opened at fourteen and a half yuan, and the retail sales of various Jiangsu and Tong japonica rice were slightly active. Prices showed little gain or loss. Those with high prices still had hope for improvement. In the South Bang area, the wholesale volume of Tao Wu was quite sufficient at noon, then slightly stabilized. Top-grade goods hovered around thirteen yuan. This product market was the least active. There was a lack of high-quality Yang Du Xian rice, and rural sales continued. The market was stable, and the Yuan Exchange went well. New arrivals were gradually being connected to large-scale purchases, and all were showing firm sales.

Silk and Tea: Last Week's Silk Market Was Dull and Lifeless 206

Overseas silk sales almost came to a standstill. Domestic silk mills' sales were not smooth.

Yokohama raw silk prices fell even more drastically. The future of the silk market is increasingly bleak.

Last week, although the party strife in the New York market subsided, it was followed by natural disasters: heavy snow and strong winds, with unusually cold weather. Major floods in Lyon were disastrous, and the economy was generally unstable. The number of silk mills that suspended operations increased daily, and raw silk sales decreased. Factory sales were stagnant, and silk prices continued to weaken. In Yokohama, sales at the three silk exchanges were halted, and prices fell even more drastically. In Shanghai, the white silk factories could not transfer to foreign firms via European telegrams, and completely stopped. Only on the weekend did inland silk mills have a slight need for medium- to low-grade yellow and white silks, but the volume was limited. The labor unrest in all Shanghai silk mills had just subsided, and only about thirty single and double palace silk mills were barely resuming work. Because the cost of silk itself was not loose, and the prices from Europe and the United States differed by two or three hundred taels, the future of the silk market became even more tragic. The entire week only saw the transaction of just over one hundred packages of Sichuan dried silk, and the price was also low. Current silk exports were just over seven hundred packages. Overseas silk prices all fell.
